B6FF 856D     09333                 STA L.PIXELCOLUMN       ; Save relative pixel column number
B701 A950     09334                 LDA #80                 ; If PLAYFIELD space object -> A := CENTERCOL = 80
B703 E005     09335                 CPX #NUMSPCOBJ.PL       ; If PLAYER space object    -> A := CENTERCOL = 125
B705 B002     09336                 BCS SKIP226             ;
B707 A97D     09337                 LDA #125                ;
              09338
B709 BCDE09   09339 SKIP226         LDY XPOSSIGN,X          ; Skip if x-coordinate positive
B70C D009     09340                 BNE SKIP227             ;
              09341
B70E 38       09342                 SEC                     ; Pixel in left screen half (x-coordinate negative)
B70F E66D     09343                 INC L.PIXELCOLUMN       ;
B711 E56D     09344                 SBC L.PIXELCOLUMN       ;
B713 9D2A0C   09345                 STA PIXELCOLUMN,X       ; Pixel column := CENTERCOL - (rel. pixel column + 1)
B716 60       09346                 RTS                     ; Return
              09347
B717 18       09348 SKIP227         CLC                     ; Pixel in right screen half (x-coordinate positive)
B718 656D     09349                 ADC L.PIXELCOLUMN       ;
B71A 9D2A0C   09350                 STA PIXELCOLUMN,X       ; Pixel column := CENTERCOL + relative pixel column
B71D 60       09351                 RTS                     ; Return
              09352
              09353 ;*******************************************************************************
              09354 ;*                                                                             *
              09355 ;*                                  SCREENROW                                  *
              09356 ;*                                                                             *
              09357 ;*          Calculate pixel row number from centered pixel row number          *
              09358 ;*                                                                             *
              09359 ;*******************************************************************************
              09360
              09361 ; Converts a pixel row number relative to the vertical screen center to a pixel
              09362 ; row number relative to the top-left corner of the screen and stores the result
              09363 ; in table PIXELROWNEW ($0BF9). The passed relative pixel row number is always
              09364 ; positive. The sign is picked from the corresponding y-component of the
              09365 ; position vector (y-coordinate).
              09366 ;
              09367 ; If the passed relative pixel row number is offscreen vertically the
              09368 ; calculation is skipped and code execution returns. If the position vector
              09369 ; corresponding to this pixel represents a PLAYFIELD space object (star,
              09370 ; explosion fragments) a new position vector is initialized in subroutine
              09371 ; INITPOSVEC ($B764) before code execution returns. If it represents a PLAYER
              09372 ; space object the PLAYER is pushed offscreen before code execution returns.
              09373 ;
              09374 ; NOTE: The vertical screen center's pixel row number for PLAYFIELD space
              09375 ; objects has a value of 50 = 100 PLAYFIELD pixels / 2. For PLAYER space objects
              09376 ; it has a value of 122 Player/Missile (PM) pixels (from top to bottom: 8 PM
              09377 ; pixels to start of Display List + 16 PM pixels to begin of PLAYFIELD + 100 PM
              09378 ; pixels to vertical screen center - 2 PM pixels (?) = 122 PM pixels).
              09379 ;
              09380 ; NOTE: If the position vector corresponding to the pixel represents a PLAYER
              09381 ; space object the passed pixel row number is doubled because 1 PLAYFIELD pixel
              09382 ; has the same height as 2 PM pixels at single-line resolution.
              09383 ;
              09384 ; When in Long-Range Scan view the z-coordinate takes the place of the
              09385 ; y-coordinate of the Front or Aft view. If the Long-Range Scan is damaged the
              09386 ; passed pixel row number is treated randomly as a negative or positive value
              09387 ; (mirror effect).
              09388 ;
              09389 ; INPUT
              09390 ;
              09391 ;   A = Pixel row number relative to the vertical screen center, always
              09392 ;       positive. Used values are:
              09393 ;     0..50 -> Regular values, pixel is onscreen
              09394 ;     $FF   -> Pixel is offscreen
              09395 ;
              09396 ;   X = Position vector index. Used values are:
              09397 ;     0..4  -> Position vector of a PLAYER space object
              09398 ;     5..48 -> Position vector of a PLAYFIELD space object
              09399
    =006D     09400 L.PIXELROW      = $6D                   ; Saves relative pixel row number
              09401
B71E C932     09402 SCREENROW       CMP #50                 ; If pixel is offscreen (A > 49)...
B720 B038     09403                 BCS SKIP233             ; ...return via initializing a new position vector
              09404
B722 856D     09405                 STA L.PIXELROW          ; Save relative pixel row number
B724 A932     09406                 LDA #50                 ; If PLAYFIELD space object -> A := CENTERROW = 50
B726 E005     09407                 CPX #NUMSPCOBJ.PL       ;
B728 B004     09408                 BCS SKIP228             ;
B72A 066D     09409                 ASL L.PIXELROW          ; If PLAYER space object -> Double pixel row number
B72C A97A     09410                 LDA #122                ; If PLAYER space object ->    A := CENTERROW = 122
              09411
B72E 24D0     09412 SKIP228         BIT SHIPVIEW            ; Skip if not in Long-Range Scan view
B730 5013     09413                 BVC SKIP230             ;
              09414
B732 2C9609   09415                 BIT GCSTATLRS           ; Skip if Long-Range Scan OK
B735 1007     09416                 BPL SKIP229             ;
              09417
B737 2C0AD2   09418                 BIT RANDOM              ; Long-Range Scan damaged...
B73A 500E     09419                 BVC SKIP231             ; ...branch randomly to pixel row number calculation
B73C 7015     09420                 BVS SKIP232             ; ...(mirror effect)
              09421
B73E BCAD09   09422 SKIP229         LDY ZPOSSIGN,X          ;
B741 D007     09423                 BNE SKIP231             ; Skip if z-coordinate pos. (Long-Range Scan view)
B743 F00E     09424                 BEQ SKIP232             ; Skip if z-coordinate neg. (Long-Range Scan view)
              09425
B745 BC0F0A   09426 SKIP230         LDY YPOSSIGN,X          ;
B748 F009     09427                 BEQ SKIP232             ; Skip if y-coordinate neg. (Front or Aft view)
              09428
B74A 38       09429 SKIP231         SEC                     ; Pixel in upper screen half (z or y coordinate pos.)
B74B E66D     09430                 INC L.PIXELROW          ;
B74D E56D     09431                 SBC L.PIXELROW          ;
B74F 9DF90B   09432                 STA PIXELROWNEW,X       ; Pixel row  := CENTERROW - (rel. pixel row + 1)
B752 60       09433                 RTS                     ; Return
              09434
B753 18       09435 SKIP232         CLC                     ; Pixel in lower screen half (y or z coordinate neg.)
B754 656D     09436                 ADC L.PIXELROW          ;
B756 9DF90B   09437                 STA PIXELROWNEW,X       ; Pixel row := CENTERROW + relative pixel row
B759 60       09438                 RTS                     ; Return
              09439
B75A E005     09440 SKIP233         CPX #NUMSPCOBJ.PL       ; Space object is offscreen. If it is a...
B75C B006     09441                 BCS INITPOSVEC          ; ...PLAYFIELD space object -> New position vector
B75E A9FB     09442                 LDA #251                ; ...PLAYER space object    -> Push PLAYER offscreen
B760 9DF90B   09443                 STA PIXELROWNEW,X       ;                              Why a value of 251 (?)
B763 60       09444 SKIP234         RTS                     ; Return
              09445
              09446 ;*******************************************************************************
              09447 ;*                                                                             *
              09448 ;*                                 INITPOSVEC                                  *
              09449 ;*                                                                             *
              09450 ;*                Initialize position vector of a space object                 *
              09451 ;*                                                                             *
              09452 ;*******************************************************************************
              09453
              09454 ; DESCRIPTION
              09455 ;
              09456 ; Initializes the position vector of a space object.
              09457 ;
              09458 ; This subroutine executes the following steps:
              09459 ;
              09460 ; (1)  Set the pixel row and column number to an offscreen value (= 99).
              09461 ;
              09462 ; (2)  If the position vector represents an explosion fragment space object then
              09463 ;      return code execution immediately. This avoids generating new explosion
              09464 ;      fragment space objects. They are separately initialized in subroutine
              09465 ;      COPYPOSVEC ($ACAF), which is called from subroutine INITEXPL ($AC6B).
              09466 ;
              09467 ; (3)  Assign default values (see below) to the position vector components
              09468 ;      (coordinates) depending on our starship's view.
              09469 ;
              09470 ; Code execution continues into subroutine RNDINVXY ($B7BE) where x and y
              09471 ; coordinates are inverted randomly.
              09472 ;
              09473 ; After passing through this and the next subroutine RNDINVXY ($B7BE) the
              09474 ; components of a position vector (coordinates) are assigned to one of the
              09475 ; following values depending on our starship's view:
              09476 ;
              09477 ; o   FRONT VIEW
              09478 ;
              09479 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+
              09480 ;     | Coordinate |                 Values                |
              09481 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+
              09482 ;     |     x      |  -4095..+4095 (-($0***)..+$0***) <KM> |
              09483 ;     |     y      |  -4095..+4095 (-($0***)..+$0***) <KM> | 
              09484 ;     |     z      |  +3840..+4095 (          +$0F**) <KM> |
              09485 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+
              09486 ;
              09487 ; o   AFT VIEW
              09488 ;
              09489 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+
              09490 ;     | Coordinate |                 Values                |
              09491 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+ 
              09492 ;     |     x      |  -3840..+3840 (-($0*00)..+$0*00) <KM> |
              09493 ;     |     y      |  -3840..+3840 (-($0*00)..+$0*00) <KM> |
              09494 ;     |     z      |  -3968.. -128 (-($0*80)        ) <KM> |
              09495 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+ 
              09496 ;     Values of x, y, and z coordinates change in increments of 256.
              09497 ;     Second digit of z-coordinate is -MAX(RNDY,RNDX), where
              09498 ;     RNDY := RND($00..$0F), RNDX := RND($00..$0F).
              09499 ;
              09500 ; o   LONG-RANGE SCAN VIEW
              09501 ;
              09502 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+
              09503 ;     | Coordinate |                 Values                |
              09504 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+
              09505 ;     |     x      | -65535..+65535 (-($****)..$****) <KM> |
              09506 ;     |     y      |  -4095..+4095  (-($0***)..$0***) <KM> |
              09507 ;     |     z      | -65535..+65535 (-($****)..$****) <KM> |
              09508 ;     +------------+---------------------------------------+
              09509 ;
              09510 ; INPUT
              09511 ;
              09512 ;   X = Position vector index. Used values are: 0..48.
              09513
    =006A     09514 L.MAXRNDXY      = $6A                   ; Saves MAX(new y-coordinate (high byte), ...
              09515                                         ;  ...new x-coordinate (high byte))
              09516
B764 A963     09517 INITPOSVEC      LDA #99                 ; Init to offscreen pixel row and column numbers
B766 9DF90B   09518                 STA PIXELROWNEW,X       ;
B769 9D2A0C   09519                 STA PIXELCOLUMN,X       ;
              09520
B76C E011     09521                 CPX #NUMSPCOBJ.NORM     ; Return if pos vector is explosion frag space obj
B76E B0F3     09522                 BCS SKIP234             ; This avoids creating new explosion frag space objs
              09523
B770 AD0AD2   09524                 LDA RANDOM              ; RNDY := RND($00..$0F)
B773 290F     09525                 AND #$0F                ;
B775 856A     09526                 STA L.MAXRNDXY          ; Save RNDY
B777 9DA20A   09527                 STA YPOSHI,X            ; y-coordinate (high byte) := RNDY
              09528
B77A AD0AD2   09529                 LDA RANDOM              ; RNDX := RND($00..$0F)
B77D 290F     09530                 AND #$0F                ;
B77F C56A     09531                 CMP L.MAXRNDXY          ;
B781 9002     09532                 BCC SKIP235             ;
B783 856A     09533                 STA L.MAXRNDXY          ; Save MAX(RNDY,RNDX)
B785 9D710A   09534 SKIP235         STA XPOSHI,X            ; x-coordinate (high byte) := RNDX
              09535
B788 A90F     09536                 LDA #$0F                ; z-coordinate (high byte) := $0F
B78A 9D400A   09537                 STA ZPOSHI,X            ;
              09538
B78D A5D0     09539                 LDA SHIPVIEW            ; z-coordinate (sign) := 1 or 0 (Front or Aft view)
B78F 4901     09540                 EOR #$01                ;
B791 2901     09541                 AND #$01                ;
B793 9DAD09   09542                 STA ZPOSSIGN,X          ;
B796 D011     09543                 BNE SKIP236             ; Skip if in Front or Long-Range Scan view
              09544
              09545                                         ; Aft view only:
B798 9D040B   09546                 STA XPOSLO,X            ; x-coordinate (low byte) := 0
B79B 9D350B   09547                 STA YPOSLO,X            ; y-coordinate (low byte) := 0
B79E 38       09548                 SEC                     ; z-coordinate (high byte) := -MAX(RNDY,RNDX)
B79F E56A     09549                 SBC L.MAXRNDXY          ;
B7A1 9D400A   09550                 STA ZPOSHI,X            ;
B7A4 A980     09551                 LDA #$80                ; z-coordinate (low byte) := $80
B7A6 9DD30A   09552                 STA ZPOSLO,X            ;
              09553
B7A9 24D0     09554 SKIP236         BIT SHIPVIEW            ; If not in Long-Range Scan view skip to RNDINVXY
B7AB 5011     09555                 BVC RNDINVXY            ;
              09556
              09557                                         ; Long-Range Scan view only:
B7AD AD0AD2   09558                 LDA RANDOM              ; x-coordinate (high byte) := RND($00..$FF)
B7B0 9D710A   09559                 STA XPOSHI,X            ;
B7B3 AD0AD2   09560                 LDA RANDOM              ; z-coordinate (high byte) := RND($00..$FF)
B7B6 9D400A   09561                 STA ZPOSHI,X            ;
B7B9 2901     09562                 AND #$01                ; Invert z-coordinate randomly
B7BB 9DAD09   09563                 STA ZPOSSIGN,X          ;
              09564
              09565 ;*******************************************************************************
              09566 ;*                                                                             *
              09567 ;*                                  RNDINVXY                                   *
              09568 ;*                                                                             *
              09569 ;*         Randomly invert the x and y components of a position vector         *
              09570 ;*                                                                             *
              09571 ;*******************************************************************************
              09572
              09573 ; DESCRIPTION
              09574 ;
              09575 ; Randomly inverts the x and y components of a position vector (x and y
              09576 ; coordinates). See also subroutine INITPOSVEC ($B764).
              09577 ;
              09578 ; INPUT
              09579 ;
              09580 ;   X = Position vector index. Used values are: 0..48.
              09581
B7BE AD0AD2   09582 RNDINVXY        LDA RANDOM              ; Set sign of y-coordinate randomly
B7C1 2901     09583                 AND #$01                ;
B7C3 9D0F0A   09584                 STA YPOSSIGN,X          ;
B7C6 D00F     09585                 BNE SKIP237             ; Skip if sign positive
              09586
B7C8 38       09587                 SEC                     ; Sign negative -> Calc negative y-coordinate
B7C9 FD350B   09588                 SBC YPOSLO,X            ; (calculate two's-complement of 16-bit value)
B7CC 9D350B   09589                 STA YPOSLO,X            ;
B7CF A900     09590                 LDA #0                  ;
B7D1 FDA20A   09591                 SBC YPOSHI,X            ;
B7D4 9DA20A   09592                 STA YPOSHI,X            ;
              09593
B7D7 AD0AD2   09594 SKIP237         LDA RANDOM              ; Set sign of x-coordinate randomly
B7DA 2901     09595                 AND #$01                ;
B7DC 9DDE09   09596                 STA XPOSSIGN,X          ;
B7DF D00F     09597                 BNE SKIP238             ; Skip if sign positive
              09598
B7E1 38       09599                 SEC                     ; Sign negative -> Calc negative x-coordinate
B7E2 FD040B   09600                 SBC XPOSLO,X            ; (calculate two's-complement of 16-bit value)
B7E5 9D040B   09601                 STA XPOSLO,X            ;
B7E8 A900     09602                 LDA #0                  ;
B7EA FD710A   09603                 SBC XPOSHI,X            ;
B7ED 9D710A   09604                 STA XPOSHI,X            ;
B7F0 60       09605 SKIP238         RTS                     ; Return
              09606
              09607 ;*******************************************************************************
              09608 ;*                                                                             *
              09609 ;*                                ISSURROUNDED                                 *
              09610 ;*                                                                             *
              09611 ;*               Check if a sector is surrounded by Zylon units                *
              09612 ;*                                                                             *
              09613 ;*******************************************************************************
              09614
              09615 ; DESCRIPTION
              09616 ;
              09617 ; Checks if a sector of the Galactic Chart is surrounded by Zylon units in the
              09618 ; adjacent NORTH, EAST, SOUTH, and WEST sectors.
              09619 ;
              09620 ; INPUT
              09621 ;
              09622 ;   X = Sector of Galactic Chart. Used values are: $00..$7F with, for example,
              09623 ;     $00 -> NORTHWEST corner sector
              09624 ;     $0F -> NORTHEAST corner sector
              09625 ;     $70 -> SOUTHWEST corner sector
              09626 ;     $7F -> SOUTHWEST corner sector
              09627 ;
              09628 ; OUTPUT
              09629 ;
              09630 ;   A = Returns if the sector is surrounded by Zylon units in the adjacent
              09631 ;       NORTH, EAST, SOUTH, and WEST sectors.
              09632 ;       0 -> Sector is not surrounded
              09633 ;     > 0 -> Sector is surrounded
              09634
B7F1 BDC808   09635 ISSURROUNDED    LDA GCMEMMAP-1,X        ; Check WEST sector
B7F4 F00D     09636                 BEQ SKIP239             ;
B7F6 BDCA08   09637                 LDA GCMEMMAP+1,X        ; Check EAST sector
B7F9 F008     09638                 BEQ SKIP239             ;
B7FB BDB908   09639                 LDA GCMEMMAP-16,X       ; Check NORTH sector
B7FE F003     09640                 BEQ SKIP239             ;
B800 BDD908   09641                 LDA GCMEMMAP+16,X       ; Check SOUTH sector
B803 60       09642 SKIP239         RTS                     ; Return
              09643
              09644 ;*******************************************************************************
              09645 ;*                                                                             *
              09646 ;*                                  UPDPANEL                                   *
              09647 ;*                                                                             *
              09648 ;*                        Update Control Panel Display                         *
              09649 ;*                                                                             *
              09650 ;*******************************************************************************
              09651
              09652 ; DESCRIPTION
              09653 ;
              09654 ; This subroutine executes the following steps: 
              09655 ;
              09656 ; (1)  Accelerate or decelerate our starship, update the VELOCITY readout
              09657 ;
              09658 ;      If the new velocity value is different from the current one either
              09659 ;      increment or decrement the current velocity value toward the new one.
              09660 ;
              09661 ;      If the Engines are damaged or destroyed (and hyperwarp is not engaged)
              09662 ;      then store a random value (less or equal than the current velocity) as
              09663 ;      the current velocity.
              09664 ;
              09665 ;      Display the updated velocity by the VELOCITY readout of the Control Panel
              09666 ;      Display.
              09667 ;
              09668 ; (2)  Update THETA, PHI, and RANGE readouts
              09669 ;
              09670 ;      If the Attack Computer is working then display the x, y, and z
              09671 ;      coordinates of the currently tracked space object as THETA, PHI, and
              09672 ;      RANGE readout values of the Control Panel Display.
              09673 ;
              09674 ; (3)  Calculate overall energy consumption
              09675 ;
              09676 ;      Add the overall energy consumption per game loop iteration to the energy
              09677 ;      counter. This value is given in energy subunits (256 energy subunits = 1
              09678 ;      energy unit displayed by the 4-digit ENERGY readout of the Console Panel
              09679 ;      Display). It is the total of the following items:
              09680 ;
              09681 ;      (1)  8 energy subunits if the Shields are up
              09682 ;
              09683 ;      (2)  2 energy subunits if the Attack Computer is on
              09684 ;
              09685 ;      (3)  1 energy subunit of the life support system
              09686 ;
              09687 ;      (4)  Our starship's Engines energy drain rate (depending on its velocity)
              09688 ;
              09689 ;      If there is a carryover of the energy counter then decrement the ENERGY
              09690 ;      readout of the Control Panel Display by one energy unit after code
              09691 ;      execution has continued into subroutine DECENERGY ($B86F). 
              09692
              09693 ;*** Accelerate or decelerate our starship *************************************
B804 A670     09694 UPDPANEL        LDX VELOCITYLO          ; Skip if new velocity = current velocity
B806 E471     09695                 CPX NEWVELOCITY         ;
B808 F008     09696                 BEQ SKIP241             ;
              09697
B80A 9004     09698                 BCC SKIP240             ; In/decrement current velocity toward new velocity
B80C C670     09699                 DEC VELOCITYLO          ;
B80E B012     09700                 BCS SKIP242             ;
B810 E670     09701 SKIP240         INC VELOCITYLO          ;
              09702
B812 A5C0     09703 SKIP241         LDA WARPSTATE           ; Skip if hyperwarp engaged
B814 D00C     09704                 BNE SKIP242             ;
              09705
B816 2C9309   09706                 BIT GCSTATENG           ; Skip if Engines are OK
B819 1007     09707                 BPL SKIP242             ;
              09708
B81B A571     09709                 LDA NEWVELOCITY         ; Store RND(0..current velocity) to current velocity
B81D 2D0AD2   09710                 AND RANDOM              ;
B820 8570     09711                 STA VELOCITYLO          ;
              09712
B822 A001     09713 SKIP242         LDY #VELOCD1-PANELTXT-1 ; Update digits of VELOCITY readout
B824 20CDB8   09714                 JSR SHOWDIGITS          ;
              09715
              09716 ;*** Display coordinates of tracked space object of Control Panel Display ******
B827 2C9509   09717                 BIT GCSTATCOM           ; Skip if Attack Computer damaged or destroyed
B82A 3030     09718                 BMI SKIP243             ;
              09719
B82C A931     09720                 LDA #$31                ; Update THETA readout (x-coordinate)
B82E A017     09721                 LDY #THETAC1-PANELTXT   ;
B830 20A7B8   09722                 JSR SHOWCOORD           ;
              09723
B833 A962     09724                 LDA #$62                ; Update PHI readout (y-coordinate)
B835 A01D     09725                 LDY #PHIC1-PANELTXT     ;
B837 20A7B8   09726                 JSR SHOWCOORD           ;
              09727
B83A A900     09728                 LDA #$00                ; Update RANGE readout (z-coordinate)
B83C A023     09729                 LDY #RANGEC1-PANELTXT   ;
B83E 20A7B8   09730                 JSR SHOWCOORD           ;
              09731
B841 AD6E09   09732                 LDA RANGEC1+2           ; Hack to clear RANGE digit 3 when in hyperwarp:
B844 8D6F09   09733                 STA RANGEC1+3           ; Copy RANGE digit 2 to digit 3
B847 C90A     09734                 CMP #CCS.9+1            ; Skip if digit character > '9' (= 'infinity' char)
B849 B011     09735                 BCS SKIP243             ;
              09736
B84B AE5C09   09737                 LDX TRACKDIGIT          ; Get z-coordinate (low byte) of tracked space object
B84E BDD30A   09738                 LDA ZPOSLO,X            ;
B851 4A       09739                 LSR A                   ; ...divide it by 16...
B852 4A       09740                 LSR A                   ;
B853 4A       09741                 LSR A                   ;
B854 4A       09742                 LSR A                   ;
B855 AA       09743                 TAX                     ;
B856 BDE90E   09744                 LDA MAPTOBCD99,X        ; ...map value of $00..$0F to BCD value 0..9
B859 8D6F09   09745                 STA RANGEC1+3           ; ...and store it to RANGE digit 3
              09746
              09747 ;*** Calculate overall energy consumption **************************************
B85C 18       09748 SKIP243         CLC                     ;
B85D A57F     09749                 LDA ENERGYCNT           ; Load energy counter
B85F 657D     09750                 ADC DRAINSHIELDS        ; Add energy drain rate of Shields
B861 6580     09751                 ADC DRAINENGINES        ; Add energy drain rate of our starship's Engines
B863 657E     09752                 ADC DRAINATTCOMP        ; Add energy drain rate of Attack Computer
B865 6901     09753                 ADC #$01                ; Add 1 energy subunit of life support system
B867 C57F     09754                 CMP ENERGYCNT           ;
B869 857F     09755                 STA ENERGYCNT           ;
B86B B039     09756                 BCS SKIP246             ; Return if no energy counter carryover
              09757
B86D A203     09758                 LDX #3                  ; Will decrement third energy digit
              09759
              09760 ;*******************************************************************************
              09761 ;*                                                                             *
              09762 ;*                                  DECENERGY                                  *
              09763 ;*                                                                             *
              09764 ;*                               Decrease energy                               *
              09765 ;*                                                                             *
              09766 ;*******************************************************************************
              09767
              09768 ; DESCRIPTION
              09769 ;
              09770 ; When not in demo mode, subtract energy from the 4-digit ENERGY readout of the
              09771 ; Control Panel Display. If crossing a 100-energy-unit boundary during
              09772 ; subtraction the score is decremented by one unit. If the energy is zero the
              09773 ; game is over.
              09774 ;
              09775 ; INPUT
              09776 ;
              09777 ;   X = ENERGY readout digit to be decremented. Used values are:
              09778 ;     1 -> Subtract 100 units from ENERGY readout
              09779 ;     2 -> Subtract  10 units from ENERGY readout
              09780 ;     3 -> Subtract   1 unit  from ENERGY readout
              09781
              09782 ;*** Display ENERGY readout ****************************************************
B86F 2464     09783 DECENERGY       BIT ISDEMOMODE          ; Return if in demo mode
B871 7033     09784                 BVS SKIP246             ;
              09785
B873 DE5509   09786                 DEC ENERGYD1,X          ; Decrement energy digit character
B876 BD5509   09787                 LDA ENERGYD1,X          ;
B879 C980     09788                 CMP #CCS.COL2!CCS.0     ;
B87B B029     09789                 BCS SKIP246             ; Return if digit character >= '0'
B87D A989     09790                 LDA #CCS.COL2!CCS.9     ;
B87F 9D5509   09791                 STA ENERGYD1,X          ; Store digit character '9'
              09792
              09793 ;*** Decrement score when crossing a 100-energy-unit boundary while subtracting 
B882 E002     09794                 CPX #2                  ; Skip if no crossing of 100-energy-unit boundary
B884 D008     09795                 BNE SKIP245             ;
              09796
B886 A5CB     09797                 LDA SCORE               ; SCORE := SCORE - 1
B888 D002     09798                 BNE SKIP244             ;
B88A C6CC     09799                 DEC SCORE+1             ;
B88C C6CB     09800 SKIP244         DEC SCORE               ;
              09801
B88E CA       09802 SKIP245         DEX                     ;
B88F 10DE     09803                 BPL DECENERGY           ; Next digit
              09804
              09805 ;*** Energy is zero, game over *************************************************
B891 A20A     09806                 LDX #CCS.SPC            ; Clear 4-digit ENERGY readout
B893 8A       09807                 TXA                     ;
B894 A003     09808                 LDY #3                  ;
B896 995509   09809 LOOP079         STA ENERGYD1,Y          ;
B899 88       09810                 DEY                     ;
B89A 10FA     09811                 BPL LOOP079             ;
              09812
B89C 2045B0   09813                 JSR SETVIEW             ; Set Front view
              09814
B89F A031     09815                 LDY #$31                ; Set title phrase "MISSION ABORTED ZERO ENERGY"
B8A1 A204     09816                 LDX #$04                ; Set mission bonus offset
B8A3 200AB1   09817                 JSR GAMEOVER            ; Game over
              09818
B8A6 60       09819 SKIP246         RTS                     ; Return
              09820
              09821 ;*******************************************************************************
              09822 ;*                                                                             *
              09823 ;*                                  SHOWCOORD                                  *
              09824 ;*                                                                             *
              09825 ;*  Display a position vector component (coordinate) in Control Panel Display  *
              09826 ;*                                                                             *
              09827 ;*******************************************************************************
              09828
              09829 ; DESCRIPTION
              09830 ;
              09831 ; Displays a position vector component (coordinate) by one of the THETA, PHI, or
              09832 ; RANGE readouts of the Control Panel Display.
              09833 ;
              09834 ; Write the sign to the Control Panel Display, then map the high byte of the
              09835 ; respective coordinate (x -> THETA, y -> PHI, z -> RANGE) to a BCD-value in
              09836 ; 00..99. Code execution continues into subroutine SHOWDIGITS ($B8CD) where the
              09837 ; digits are actually stored in the Control Panel Display.
              09838 ;
              09839 ; NOTE: If the digits of either the THETA or PHI readout are to be displayed and
              09840 ; the x or y position vector component (high byte) is $FF then tweak the value
              09841 ; to $FE. This avoids accessing table MAPTOBCD99 ($0EE9) with an index of $FF
              09842 ; that would return the special value $EA. This value represents the CCS.INF
              09843 ; ($0E) and CCS.SPC ($0A) characters (see comments in subroutine INITIALIZE
              09844 ; ($B3BA)) that are displayed by the RANGE readout only.
              09845 ;
              09846 ; INPUT
              09847 ;
              09848 ;   A = Position vector component (coordinate) offset. Used values are: 
              09849 ;     $00 -> z-coordinate
              09850 ;     $31 -> x-coordinate
              09851 ;     $62 -> y-coordinate
              09852 ;
              09853 ;   Y = Offset into the Control Panel Display memory map. Used values are:
              09854 ;     $17 -> First character (sign) of THETA readout (x-coordinate of tracked
              09855 ;            space object)
              09856 ;     $1D -> First character (sign) of PHI readout   (y-coordinate of tracked
              09857 ;            space object)
              09858 ;     $23 -> First character (sign) of RANGE readout (z-coordinate of tracked
              09859 ;            space object)
              09860
    =006A     09861 L.SIGNCHAR      = $6A                   ; Saves sign character
              09862
B8A7 18       09863 SHOWCOORD       CLC                     ; Add index of tracked space object...
B8A8 6D5C09   09864                 ADC TRACKDIGIT          ; ...to position vector component offset
B8AB AA       09865                 TAX                     ; Save position vector component index
              09866
              09867 ;*** Display sign in Control Panel Display *************************************
B8AC A910     09868                 LDA #CCS.PLUS           ; Save '+' (CCS.PLUS) to sign character
B8AE 856A     09869                 STA L.SIGNCHAR          ;
              09870
B8B0 BDAD09   09871                 LDA ZPOSSIGN,X          ; Prep sign of coordinate
B8B3 4A       09872                 LSR A                   ;
B8B4 BD400A   09873                 LDA ZPOSHI,X            ; Prep coordinate (high byte)
B8B7 B004     09874                 BCS SKIP247             ; Skip if sign is positive
              09875
B8B9 49FF     09876                 EOR #$FF                ; Invert coordinate (high byte)
B8BB C66A     09877                 DEC L.SIGNCHAR          ; Change saved sign character to '-' (CCS.MINUS)
              09878
B8BD AA       09879 SKIP247         TAX                     ; Save coordinate (high byte)
B8BE A56A     09880                 LDA L.SIGNCHAR          ; Store sign character in Control Panel Display
B8C0 994909   09881                 STA PANELTXT,Y          ;
              09882
              09883 ;*** Get RANGE digits **********************************************************
B8C3 98       09884                 TYA                     ; Skip if RANGE is to be displayed
B8C4 2910     09885                 AND #$10                ;
B8C6 F005     09886                 BEQ SHOWDIGITS          ;
              09887
B8C8 E0FF     09888                 CPX #$FF                ; If coordinate (high byte) = $FF decrement value
B8CA D001     09889                 BNE SHOWDIGITS          ; This avoids output of CCS.INFINITY in...
B8CC CA       09890                 DEX                     ; ...THETA and PHI readouts
              09891
              09892 ;*******************************************************************************
              09893 ;*                                                                             *
              09894 ;*                                 SHOWDIGITS                                  *
              09895 ;*                                                                             *
              09896 ;*          Display a value by a readout of the Control Panel Display          *
              09897 ;*                                                                             *
              09898 ;*******************************************************************************
              09899
              09900 ; DESCRIPTION
              09901 ;
              09902 ; Converts a binary value in $00..$FF to a BCD-value in 0..99 and displays it as
              09903 ; a 2-digit number in the Control Panel Display.
              09904 ;
              09905 ; INPUT
              09906 ;
              09907 ;   X = Value to be displayed as a 2-digit BCD-value. Used values are: $00..$FF.
              09908 ;
              09909 ;   Y = Offset into the Control Panel Display memory map relative to the first
              09910 ;       character of the Control Panel Display (the 'V' of the VELOCITY
              09911 ;       readout). Used values are: 
              09912 ;     $01 -> Character before first digit of VELOCITY readout
              09913 ;     $17 -> First character (sign) of THETA readout (x-coordinate of tracked
              09914 ;            space object)
              09915 ;     $1D -> First character (sign) of PHI readout   (y-coordinate of tracked
              09916 ;            space object)
              09917 ;     $23 -> First character (sign) of RANGE readout (z-coordinate of tracked
              09918 ;            space object)
              09919
B8CD BDE90E   09920 SHOWDIGITS      LDA MAPTOBCD99,X        ; Map binary value to BCD-value
B8D0 AA       09921                 TAX                     ;
B8D1 290F     09922                 AND #$0F                ;
B8D3 994B09   09923                 STA PANELTXT+2,Y        ; Store 'ones' digit in Control Panel Display
B8D6 8A       09924                 TXA                     ;
B8D7 4A       09925                 LSR A                   ;
B8D8 4A       09926                 LSR A                   ;
B8D9 4A       09927                 LSR A                   ;
B8DA 4A       09928                 LSR A                   ;
B8DB 994A09   09929                 STA PANELTXT+1,Y        ; Store 'tens' digit in Control Panel Display
B8DE 60       09930                 RTS                     ; Return
              09931
              09932 ;*******************************************************************************
              09933 ;*                                                                             *
              09934 ;*                G A M E   D A T A   ( P A R T   2   O F   2 )                *
              09935 ;*                                                                             *
              09936 ;*******************************************************************************
              09937
              09938 ;*** Color register offsets of PLAYER0..4 **************************************
B8DF 00       09939 PLCOLOROFFTAB   .BYTE 0                               ; PLAYER0
B8E0 01       09940                 .BYTE 1                               ; PLAYER1
B8E1 02       09941                 .BYTE 2                               ; PLAYER2
B8E2 03       09942                 .BYTE 3                               ; PLAYER3
B8E3 07       09943                 .BYTE 7                               ; PLAYER4
              09944
              09945 ;*** Shape table 1 (PLAYER2..4) ************************************************
B8E4 00       09946 PLSHAP1TAB      .BYTE $00                             ; ........
B8E5 18       09947                 .BYTE $18                             ; ...##...
B8E6 3C       09948                 .BYTE $3C                             ; ..####..
B8E7 7E       09949                 .BYTE $7E                             ; .######.
B8E8 7E       09950                 .BYTE $7E                             ; .######.
B8E9 76       09951                 .BYTE $76                             ; .###.##.
B8EA F7       09952                 .BYTE $F7                             ; ####.###
B8EB DF       09953                 .BYTE $DF                             ; ##.#####
B8EC DF       09954                 .BYTE $DF                             ; ##.#####
B8ED FF       09955                 .BYTE $FF                             ; ########
B8EE FF       09956                 .BYTE $FF                             ; ########

              10497 ;*** 3-byte elements to draw cross hairs and Attack Computer Display ***********
              10498 ;   Byte 1 : Pixel column number of line start
              10499 ;   Byte 2 : Pixel row number of line start
              10500 ;   Byte 3 : B7 = 0 -> Draw line to the right
              10501 ;            B7 = 1 -> Draw line down
              10502 ;            B6..0  -> Length of line in pixels. Possible values are: 0..127.
              10503 ;
              10504 ;                   #
              10505 ;                   #                              4
              10506 ;                   #                      ##############################
              10507 ;                   #1                     #             #              #
              10508 ;                   #                      #             #11            #
              10509 ;                   #                      #             #              #
              10510 ;                   #                      #5            #    8         #6
              10511 ;                                          #      ###############       #
              10512 ;                                          #      #             #       #
              10513 ;         15                  16           #   7  #             #   10  #
              10514 ; ###############       ###############    ########             #########
              10515 ;                                          #      #12           #       #
              10516 ;                                          #      #             #13     #
              10517 ;                                          #      ###############       #
              10518 ;                   #                      #         9   #              #
              10519 ;                   #                      #             #              #
              10520 ;                   #                      #             #14            #
              10521 ;                   #                      #       3     #              #
              10522 ;                   #2                     ##############################
              10523 ;                   #
              10524 ;                   #
              10525 ;
              10526 ;         Front/Aft Cross Hairs                Attack Computer Display
              10527 ;
              10528 ; LOCAL VARIABLES
    =0080     10529 DOWN            = $80
    =0000     10530 RIGHT           = $00

              10567
              10568 ;*** Initial x and y coordinates of a star during hyperwarp ********************
              10569 ; The following two tables are used to determine the initial x and y coordinates
              10570 ; (high byte) of a star during hyperwarp. An index in 0..3 picks both the x and
              10571 ; y coordinate, thus 4 pairs of coordinates are possible:
              10572 ;
              10573 ; Y           +-------+----------------------------+----------------------------+
              10574 ; ^           | Index |        x-coordinate        |        y-coordinate        |
              10575 ; |           +-------+----------------------------+----------------------------+
              10576 ; |.32.       |   0   | +1024..+1279 (+$04**) <KM> |  +512..+767  (+$02**) <KM> |
              10577 ; |...1       |   1   | +1024..+1279 (+$04**) <KM> |  +768..+1023 (+$03**) <KM> |
              10578 ; |...0       |   2   |  +768..+1023 (+$03**) <KM> | +1024..+1279 (+$04**) <KM> |
              10579 ; |....       |   3   |  +512..+767  (+$02**) <KM> | +1024..+1279 (+$04**) <KM> |
              10580 ; 0----->X    +-------+----------------------------+----------------------------+
              10581
              10582 ;*** Initial x-coordinate (high byte) of star in hyperwarp *********************
BB3A 04       10583 WARPSTARXTAB    .BYTE $04                             ; +1024..+1279 (+$04**) <KM>
BB3B 04       10584                 .BYTE $04                             ; +1024..+1279 (+$04**) <KM>
BB3C 03       10585                 .BYTE $03                             ;  +768..+1023 (+$03**) <KM>
BB3D 02       10586                 .BYTE $02                             ;  +512..+767  (+$02**) <KM>
              10587
              10588 ;*** Initial y-coordinate (high byte) of star in hyperwarp *********************
BB3E 02       10589 WARPSTARYTAB    .BYTE $02                             ;  +512..+767  (+$02**) <KM>
BB3F 03       10590                 .BYTE $03                             ;  +768..+1023 (+$03**) <KM>
BB40 04       10591                 .BYTE $04                             ; +1024..+1279 (+$04**) <KM>
BB41 04       10592                 .BYTE $04                             ; +1024..+1279 (+$04**) <KM>

              11209 ; (9) AUDCTL        ($D208) POKEY: Audio control

              11216 ; (2) NOISEAUDF2    ($DF)   Audio channel 2 frequency shadow register
              11217 ; (1) NOISEFRQINC   ($E0)   Audio channel 1/2 frequency increment

              11225 ;*** 5 x 6-byte beeper sound patterns (bytes 0..5 stored in reverse order) *****
              11226 ;
              11227 ; (5) BEEPFRQIND    ($D2) Running index into frequency table BEEPFRQTAB ($BF5C)
              11228 ; (4) BEEPREPEAT    ($D3) Number of times the beeper sound pattern sequence is repeated - 1
              11229 ; (3) BEEPTONELIFE  ($D4) Lifetime of tone in TICKs - 1
              11230 ; (2) BEEPPAUSELIFE ($D5) Lifetime of pause in TICKs - 1 ($FF -> No pause)
              11231 ; (1) BEEPPRIORITY  ($D6) Beeper sound pattern priority. A playing beeper sound pattern is
              11232 ;                         stopped if a beeper sound pattern of higher priority is about to be
              11233 ;                         played. A value of 0 indicates that no beeper sound pattern is
              11234 ;                         playing at the moment.
              11235 ; (0) BEEPFRQSTART  ($D7) Index to first byte of the beeper sound pattern frequency in table
              11236 ;                         BEEPFRQTAB ($BF5C)
